#####		Colonial First Wave Bounce Events (Ai)	610-619		#####

country_event = {
    id = 777770610
    title = "Our colony may be transfered?"
    desc = "Our lands may be transfered though dismantlement."

    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 0.99 }

							}

					}
				}

#####		Colonial Dismantlement Leader Decision Events	620-629		#####

country_event = {
    id = 777770620
    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is controlled by the defeated power, what should be done with it?"
	picture = "dismantle 8"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship }OR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { #####		Colonial Primary Effect Bouncing Events	640-649		#####

country_event = {
    id = 777770640
    title = "Our colony is being considered?"
    desc = "Our colony is being considered by the Conference Chair!"
	picture = "dismantle 12"
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } } 
				has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor
			}
			FROM = { country_event = 777770750 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {

			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						province_id = 1814

					}
				}

				add_core = UTI
			}

		}

			owner = { UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } } }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { any_owned_province = { NOT = { is_core = UTI } } } check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } } }
			owner = { annex_to = UTI UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } } }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { any_owned_province = { NOT = { is_core = UTI } } check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } } }
			owner = {
				any_owned = { limit = { is_core = UTI is_core = THIS } remove_core = THIS add_core = CLN }
				release = UTI
				UTI = { annex_to = UTI any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CLN } add_core = THIS remove_core = CLN } all_core = { remove_core = UTI } }
			}
		}
		random_country = {

				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } }
			}
			inherit = UTI

		random_country = {

			}

		}

		UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } }
		
		THIS = { set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0 } }
    }

		}

    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is controlled by the defeated power, what should be done with it?"
	picture = "dismantle 13"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship }OR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Presidential_Dictatorship }OR = { government = fascist_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Fascist_Dictatorship } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Presidential_Dictatorship }OR = { government = fascist_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Fascist_Dictatorship } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = absolute_monarchy has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Monarchy }OR = { government = absolute_empire has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Empire }OR = { government = semi_constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Semi_Constitutional_Empire } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = absolute_monarchy has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Monarchy }OR = { government = absolute_empire has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Empire }OR = { government = semi_constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Semi_Constitutional_Empire } } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism }OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship }OR = { government = parliamentary_republic has_country_flag = Government_Parliamentary_Republic }OR = { government = prussian_constitutionalism has_country_flag = Government_Prussian_Constitutionalism } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Presidential_Dictatorship }OR = { government = fascist_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Fascist_Dictatorship } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Presidential_Dictatorship }OR = { government = fascist_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Fascist_Dictatorship } } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = {OR = { government = absolute_monarchy has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Monarchy }OR = { government = absolute_empire has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Empire }OR = { government = semi_constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Semi_Constitutional_Empire } } } THIS = { OR = {OR = { government = absolute_monarchy has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Monarchy }OR = { government = absolute_empire has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Empire }OR = { government = semi_constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Semi_Constitutional_Empire } } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
	
    option = {
        name = "We shall offer $FROMCOUNTRY$ to other victors."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Give_Away_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 OR = {OR = { government = hms_government has_country_flag = Government_Hms_Government }OR = { government = constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Constitutional_Empire }OR = { government = absolute_monarchy has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Monarchy }OR = { government = absolute_empire has_country_flag = Government_Absolute_Empire }OR = { government = semi_constitutional_empire has_country_flag = Government_Semi_Constitutional_Empire } } }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall remain with the defeated."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = As_Is_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall exist as an independent state."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Independent_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "Integrate $FROMCOUNTRY$ into Ethiopia"
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Ethiopia_Colony_Choice value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "Integrate $FROMCOUNTRY$ into Somalia"
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Somalia_Colony_Choice value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracyOR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship has_country_flag = Government_Proletarian_Dictatorship } } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
}

				tag = FROM

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }

		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM

					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war

			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }

				tag = FROM
			}
